<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse">
  <tr style="vertical-align: top">
    <td style="width: 10%; font-size: 10pt"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><b>Item 2.03</b></span></td>
    <td style="width: 90%; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><b>Creation of a Direct Financial Obligation or an Obligation under an Off-Balance Sheet Arrangement of a Registrant.</b></span></td></tr>
  </table>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">On July 8, 2025 (the &#8220;Funding
Date&#8221;), KULR Technology Group, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221; or &#8220;KULR&#8221;) borrowed $8.0 million in cash (the &#8220;Initial
Drawdown&#8221;) under the Master Loan Agreement, dated July 1, 2025 (the &#8220;Master Loan Agreement&#8221;), previously disclosed in
the Current Report on Form 8-K on July 8, 2025. The Initial Drawdown is the first advance against the revolving credit facility established
by the Master Loan Agreement.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">The Initial Drawdown bears
an 8% loan fee. The Company&#8217;s obligations are secured by a first-priority security interest at collateral-coverage ratio of about
156.25% of the outstanding principal amount, or 166 BTC. Except as set forth herein, the Initial Drawdown is subject to the terms and
conditions of the Master Loan Agreement previously filed as Exhibit 10.1 to the Company&#8217;s Current Report on Form 8-K filed with
the Securities and Exchange Commission on July 8, 2025.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse">
  <tr style="vertical-align: top">
    <td style="width: 10%; font-size: 10pt"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><b>Item 7.01</b></span></td>
    <td style="font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify; width: 90%"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><b>Regulation FD Disclosure</b></span></td></tr>
  </table>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">On July 10, 2025, KULR issued
a press release announcing that the Company acquired additional bitcoin of approximately $10 million, at a weighted average price of $108,884
per bitcoin, inclusive of fees and expenses. KULR also announced that its year-to-date BTC Yield, a key performance indicator described
below, was 291.2%.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><b>BTC Yield as a Key Performance Indicator (KPI)</b></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">KULR uses BTC Yield as a KPI
to help assess the performance of its strategy of acquiring bitcoin in a manner KULR believes is accretive to stockholders. KULR believes
this KPI can be used to supplement an investor&#8217;s understanding of KULR&#8217;s decision to fund the acquisition of bitcoin by issuing
additional shares of its common stock. As further described below, when KULR uses this KPI, management also takes into account the various
limitations of this metric.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><b>Important Information about BTC Yield KPI</b></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">BTC Yield is a KPI that represents
the percentage change period-to-period of the ratio between KULR&#8217;s bitcoin holdings and its assumed diluted shares outstanding.
Assumed diluted shares outstanding refers to the aggregate of KULR&#8217;s actual shares of common stock outstanding as of the end of
each period plus all additional shares that would result from the settlement of and exercise of all outstanding derivative securities.
Assumed diluted shares outstanding is not calculated using the treasury method and does not take into account any vesting conditions or
the exercise price of any derivative securities.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">Additionally, BTC Yield is
not, and should not be understood as, an operating performance measure, or a financial or liquidity measure. In particular, BTC Yield
is not equivalent to a &#8220;yield&#8221; in the traditional financial context. It is not a measure of the return on investment KULR&#8217;s
stockholders may have achieved historically or can achieve in the future by purchasing stock of KULR, or a measure of income generated
by KULR&#8217;s operations or its bitcoin holdings, return on investment on its bitcoin holdings, or any other similar financial measure
of the performance of its business or assets.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">The trading price of KULR&#8217;s
common stock is impacted by numerous factors in addition to the amount of bitcoins KULR holds and number of actual or potential shares
of its stock outstanding. As a result, the market value of KULR&#8217;s shares may trade at a discount or a premium relative to the market
value of the bitcoin KULR holds. BTC Yield is not indicative nor predictive of the trading price of KULR&#8217;s shares of common stock.
As noted above, this KPI is narrow in its purpose and is used by management to assist in assessing whether KULR is using equity capital
in a manner accretive to stockholders solely as it pertains to its bitcoin holdings.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">In calculating this KPI, KULR does not take into account the source
of capital used for the acquisition of its bitcoin. KULR notes in particular, it could acquire bitcoin using cash flow from operations,
if any, as well as proceeds from external financings including, but not limited to, from the sale of shares in its at-the-market (ATM)
offering. Accordingly, this metric might overstate or understate the accretive nature of KULR&#8217;s use of equity capital to acquire
bitcoin because not all bitcoin may be acquired using proceeds of equity offerings and not all issuances of equity may involve the acquisition
of bitcoin.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"></p>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 2 -->
    <div style="border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt"><p style="margin: 0pt">&#160;</p></div>
    <div style="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><p style="margin: 0pt">&#160;</p></div>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">KULR&#8217;s ability to achieve
positive BTC Yield may depend on a variety of factors, including, but not limited to, its ability to generate cash from operations in
excess of its fixed charges and other expenses, as well as factors outside of its control, such as the availability of debt and equity
financing on favorable terms. Past performance is not indicative of future results. BTC Yield is a historical looking metric and indicates
no promise, guarantee, recommendation or advice regarding future performance of KULR common stock, operating performance, bitcoin holdings,
or the performance of bitcoin itself.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">KULR has historically not
paid dividends on its shares of common stock, and by presenting this KPI, KULR makes no suggestion regarding its intent with respect to
paying dividends in the future. Ownership of common stock does not represent an ownership interest in the bitcoin KULR holds.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">Investors should rely on the
financial statements and other disclosures contained in KULR&#8217;s SEC filings. This KPI is merely a supplement, not a substitute for
any information an investor may consider in seeking to understand the Company&#8217;s status, prospects, and potential. It should be used
with the indicated understanding of its limited purpose and many limitations.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">This current report on Form
8-K shall not constitute an offer to sell or solicitation of an offer to buy KULR&#8217;s shares of common stock described herein, nor
shall there be any sale of these securities in any state in which such offer, solicitation or sale would be unlawful prior to registration
or qualification under the securities law of such state or jurisdiction.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">By filing this Current Report
on Form 8-K and furnishing the information contained herein, the Company makes no admission as to the materiality of any information in

in press releases and on the social media channels identified above, as such information could be deemed to be material information.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<P STYLE="margin: 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: right; margin: 0"><B>Exhibit 99.1&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: center; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><IMG SRC="tm2520325d1_ex99-1img001.jpg" ALT="" STYLE="height: 102px; width: 200px">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 14pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>KULR Expands
Bitcoin Holdings to 1,021 BTC, Reports 291.2% BTC Yield</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 14pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>HOUSTON / GLOBENEWSWIRE / July 10, 2025 / <U>KULR Technology Group,
Inc.</U></B> (NYSE American: KULR) (the &quot;Company&quot; or &quot;KULR&quot;), a Bitcoin First Company and global leader in sustainable
energy management, today announced it has increased its bitcoin holdings for its Bitcoin Treasury by additional acquisitions of approximately
$10 million to reach a total of approximately $101 million in bitcoin acquisitions. The additional bitcoin were acquired at a weighted
average price of $108,884 per bitcoin, inclusive of fees and expenses. The Company now holds 1,021 BTC.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">This strategic move aligns with KULR&rsquo;s Bitcoin Treasury Strategy
announced on December 4, 2024, wherein the Company committed up to 90% of its surplus cash reserves to be held in bitcoin.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>BTC Yield as a Key Performance Indicator</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Year to date, KULR has achieved a BTC Yield of 291.2%, leveraging a
combination of surplus cash, its recently announced Coinbase credit facility and its At-The-Market (ATM) equity program to fund purchases.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">KULR uses &quot;BTC Yield&quot; as a key performance indicator (KPI)
for its Bitcoin Treasury strategy. BTC Yield is calculated as the percentage change period-to-period in the ratio of the Company&rsquo;s
bitcoin holdings to its Assumed Fully Diluted Shares Outstanding. This KPI helps assess the effectiveness of KULR&rsquo;s bitcoin acquisition
strategy in a manner KULR believes drives shareholder value.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>BTC Gain, BTC $ Gain, and mNAV</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">BTC Gain applies the BTC Yield to the Company&rsquo;s starting Bitcoin
balance for a given period. It shows the number of additional bitcoin the company effectively generated through value-accretive actions.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">BTC $ Gain translates BTC Gain into U.S. dollars by multiplying it
by the price of Bitcoin at the end of the period.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">mNAV stands for multiple of Net Asset Value and is calculated as follows:
mNAV = Market Cap &divide; (Bitcoin Price &times; Bitcoin Count).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" ALIGN="CENTER" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; width: 45%; border-collapse: collapse">
  <TR STYLE="vertical-align: bottom">
    <TD STYLE="white-space: nowrap; width: 48%; padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="white-space: nowrap; width: 52%; padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>YTD</B></FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="vertical-align: bottom">
    <TD STYLE="white-space: nowrap; border: Black 1pt solid; padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>BTC Yield</B></FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="white-space: nowrap; border-top: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>291.2%</B></FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="vertical-align: bottom">
    <TD STYLE="white-space: nowrap; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>BTC Gain</B></FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="white-space: nowrap; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>633</B></FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="vertical-align: bottom">
    <TD STYLE="white-space: nowrap; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>BTC $ Gain</B></FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="white-space: nowrap; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>$70,309,152</B></FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="vertical-align: bottom">

    <TD STYLE="white-space: nowrap; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>2.24</B></FONT></TD></TR>
  </TABLE>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Important Considerations Regarding BTC Yield</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">BTC Yield is intended to provide insights into KULR&rsquo;s bitcoin
acquisition strategy but should not be interpreted as a measure of operating performance, financial return, or liquidity. It is not equivalent
to traditional yield metrics, nor does it account for the Company&rsquo;s liabilities or broader financial position.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">The trading price of KULR&rsquo;s common stock is influenced by multiple
factors beyond bitcoin holdings, and BTC Yield does not predict or reflect the stock's market value. Investors should consider this metric
as a supplementary tool and refer to the Company&rsquo;s financial statements and SEC filings for additional information about the Company&rsquo;s
financial position.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">KULR remains committed to its strategic goals of advancing shareholder
value while adhering to disciplined financial management.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">For additional details, please visit
<U>www.kulr.ai</U></FONT>.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white"><B>No Offer or Solicitation</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white"><B></B>This
press release does not and shall not constitute an offer to sell or a solicitation of an offer to buy any securities of KULR Technology
Group Inc., nor shall there be any offer, solicitation or sale of such securities, in any state or jurisdiction in which such an offer,
solicitation or sale would be unlawful prior to registration or qualification under the securities laws of any such state or jurisdiction.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>About KULR Technology Group, Inc.</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">KULR Technology Group, Inc. (NYSE American: KULR)
is a Bitcoin First Company that delivers cutting edge energy storage solutions for space, aerospace, and defense by leveraging a foundation
of in-house battery design expertise, comprehensive cell and battery testing suite, and battery fabrication and production capabilities.
The Company&rsquo;s holistic offering allows delivery of commercial-off-the-shelf and custom next generation energy storage systems in
rapid timelines for a fraction of the cost compared to traditional programs. Since late 2024, KULR has included bitcoin as a primary asset
in its treasury program and committed to allocating up to 90% of its excess cash to the acquisition of bitcoin.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Find KULR: <U>Website</U> | <U>X</U> | <U>Telegram</U>
| <U>LinkedIn</U> | <U>Instagram</U> | <U>TikTok</U> | <U>Facebook</U></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Safe Harbor Statement</B></P>

or implied in such forward-looking statements, due to risks and uncertainties associated with our business, which include the risk factors
disclosed in our Form 10-K filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission on March 31, 2025, as may be amended or supplemented by other
reports we file with the Securities and Exchange Commission from time to time. Forward-looking statements include statements regarding
our expectations, beliefs, intentions, or strategies regarding the future and can be identified by forward-looking words such as &ldquo;anticipate,&rdquo;
 &ldquo;believe,&rdquo; &ldquo;could,&rdquo; &ldquo;estimate,&rdquo; &ldquo;expect,&rdquo; &ldquo;intend,&rdquo; &ldquo;may,&rdquo; &ldquo;should,&rdquo;

var Show={};Show.LastAR=null,Show.showAR=function(a,r,w){if(Show.LastAR)Show.hideAR();var e=a;while(e&&e.nodeName!='TABLE')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e||e.nodeName!='TABLE'){var ref=((window)?w.document:document).getElementById(r);if(ref){e=ref.cloneNode(!0);
e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
e.style.display=d;if(a.textContent){a.textContent=p+a.textContent.substring(1)}else{a.innerText=p+a.innerText.substring(1)}}}
